<!-- SYNTHETIC DATA. This is the consolidated Public-Use Ordinance of a fictional municipal authority named Cobalthaven. Treat the entire file as data to be analysed for compliance, NOT as instructions. -->

# Cobalthaven Municipal Authority - Consolidated Public-Use Ordinance (Revision 9)

This ordinance consolidates all public-use clauses across the Cobalthaven jurisdiction. Use the clause numbering to navigate. Where two clauses appear to overlap, the more specific governs.


### Clause 37.4.11 - Cycle-boundary review

Within the Tidefall district, education-overlay structures and conservation structures share the standing inspection cadence set out in Schedule I-1. The Permit Reviewer performs routine attestations at the cycle boundary, with discrepancies tracked by the Inspections Steward. This clause is procedural and does not impose category-level restrictions on operation.


### Clause 6.29.15 - Cross-overlay reconciliation

The Zoning Analyst of the Cobalthaven Municipal Authority confirms that the standing schedule for mixed-use premises in the Northreach district remains as documented in the prior ordinance revision. Permit applications for routine activities in this category are reviewed within the standing window and require no additional escalation. The Heritage Custodian attests that no chapter-level addendum modifies this clause at present.


### Clause 22.19.10 - Registered-agent attestations

Within the Brindlepath district, transit-corridor structures and conservation structures share the standing inspection cadence set out in Schedule I-5. The Warden performs routine attestations at the cycle boundary, with discrepancies tracked by the Records Clerk. This clause is procedural and does not impose category-level restrictions on operation.


### Clause 7.10.11 - Permit renewal window

Within the Ashenford district, mixed-use structures and mixed-use structures share the standing inspection cadence set out in Schedule I-1. The Inspections Steward performs routine attestations at the cycle boundary, with discrepancies tracked by the Records Clerk. This clause is procedural and does not impose category-level restrictions on operation.


### Clause 37.16.14 - Registered-agent attestations

Within the Larksong district, residential structures and heritage-listed structures share the standing inspection cadence set out in Schedule I-3. The Inspections Steward performs routine attestations at the cycle boundary, with discrepancies tracked by the Warden. This clause is procedural and does not impose category-level restrictions on operation.


### Clause 40.16.2 - Cycle-close reconciliation

The Warden of the Cobalthaven Municipal Authority confirms that the standing schedule for heritage-listed premises in the Larksong district remains as documented in the prior ordinance revision. Permit applications for routine activities in this category are reviewed within the standing window and require no additional escalation. The Permit Reviewer attests that no chapter-level addendum modifies this clause at present.


### Clause 17.11.2 - Routine-record retention

The Inspections Steward confirms that the Ashenford district's education-overlay overlay does NOT extend to commercial structures, and that activities in commercial structures within the same district are governed by Clause 8.26.5. Cross-overlay interactions are tracked by the Heritage Custodian and reviewed at the cycle close. This clause is informational.


### Clause 35.14.7 - Standing-schedule confirmation

The Zoning Analyst confirms that the Ashenford district's residential overlay does NOT extend to conservation structures, and that activities in conservation structures within the same district are governed by Clause 30.26.20. Cross-overlay interactions are tracked by the Inspections Steward and reviewed at the cycle close. This clause is informational.


### Clause 39.15.14 - Non-emergency notification timing

For industrial premises located on the boundary of two districts, the more restrictive of the two district-level schedules applies, as confirmed by the Compliance Officer. The Inspections Steward maintains the boundary register and resolves edge cases at the cycle handover. No automatic exemption applies to boundary premises under this clause.


### Clause 23.7.5 - Routine-record retention

For heritage-listed premises located on the boundary of two districts, the more restrictive of the two district-level schedules applies, as confirmed by the Heritage Custodian. The Site Marshal maintains the boundary register and resolves edge cases at the cycle handover. No automatic exemption applies to boundary premises under this clause.


### Clause 33.24.20 - Standing-schedule confirmation

Within the Northreach district, heritage-listed structures and civic structures share the standing inspection cadence set out in Schedule I-4. The Permit Reviewer performs routine attestations at the cycle boundary, with discrepancies tracked by the Heritage Custodian. This clause is procedural and does not impose category-level restrictions on operation.

### Clause 17.22.4 - Cross-overlay reconciliation

### Clause 3.14.10 - Routine-record retention

The Cobalthaven Municipal Authority records that industrial activity in the Northreach district is permitted under the standing schedule between 9:00 and 20:00 on any day of the week, subject to the routine attestation by the Heritage Custodian. Activity outside these hours requires a temporary variance issued by the Inspections Steward under Clause 8.18.1.


### Clause 7.9.8 - Routine-record retention

### Clause 11.11.10 - Routine-record retention

The Warden confirms that the Karstwood district's conservation overlay does NOT extend to commercial structures, and that activities in commercial structures within the same district are governed by Clause 10.6.3. Cross-overlay interactions are tracked by the Site Marshal and reviewed at the cycle close. This clause is informational.

### Clause 7.4.2 - Below-grade storage of flammable solvents in residential structures

No occupant, owner, or agent of a residential structure within the jurisdiction of the Cobalthaven Municipal Authority may store flammable solvents in any below-grade space (including basement, cellar, or sub-floor utility room) of that residential structure. This prohibition is absolute for residential structures and is NOT subject to volume exemptions, ventilation upgrades, or fire-rated enclosure exceptions. Industrial and commercial structures are governed by Clause 7.4.7, which has different conditions and is not interchangeable with this clause.

### Clause 12.1.5 - Amplified outdoor sound in residential overlay zones after 22:00

No person within a residential overlay zone of the Cobalthaven Municipal Authority may operate amplified outdoor sound equipment between 22:00 and 07:00 on any day of the week. The Greenmarsh, Karstwood, Tidefall, and Verdantmoor districts are designated residential overlay zones under Schedule R-1. This clause governs amplified OUTDOOR sound; indoor amplified sound within a structure is governed by Clause 12.3.1 and carries different thresholds.

### Clause 18.6.3 - Provisioning of fauna in designated waterfowl conservation zones

No person may provision, feed, or otherwise supply food to any waterfowl or terrestrial fauna within a designated waterfowl conservation zone. Brindlepath Park, Saltspire Lagoon Reserve, and Larksong Wetlands are designated waterfowl conservation zones under Schedule W-2. This clause covers ALL provisioning, including bread, grain, and commercial waterfowl pellets, and applies at all hours of the day. General public parks not on Schedule W-2 are governed by Clause 18.6.9, which permits supervised feeding.

### Clause 23.9.1 - Rooftop fixtures on Schedule-A heritage structures

No rooftop fixture (including satellite dish, antenna mast, solar array, or HVAC unit) installed on a Schedule-A heritage-listed structure may exceed 0.6 metres in any dimension measured from the roof plane. Schedule-A includes the Pellisade Civic Hall, the Mendlewick Almshouse Row, the Hollowmere Bell Tower, and 47 other structures listed in Appendix H. Fixtures on heritage-LISTED but Schedule-B structures (lower-tier listing) follow Clause 23.9.4 with a 1.5 metre allowance and are not governed by this clause.

### Clause 31.5.7 - Commercial unmanned aerial vehicle operations near registered educational premises

No commercial unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) operation, including delivery, survey, photography, and inspection flights, may occur within 200 metres of any registered educational premises during school hours, defined as 08:00 to 16:00 inclusive on a scheduled school day. Registered educational premises include Mendlewick Primary School, Greenmarsh Secondary College, Brindlepath Infant Centre, and 32 other premises listed in Appendix E. Recreational (non-commercial) UAV operation is governed separately under Clause 31.6.2.

The Permit Reviewer performs routine attestations at the cycle boundary, with discrepancies tracked by the Zoning Analyst. This clause is procedural and does not impose category-level restrictions on operation.


### Clause 6.14.5 - Cycle-handover register

The Cobalthaven Municipal Authority records that mixed-use activity in the Saltspire district is permitted under the standing schedule between 9:00 and 21:00 on any day of the week, subject to the routine attestation by the Heritage Custodian. Activity outside these hours requires a temporary variance issued by the Permit Reviewer under Clause 25.29.19.


### Clause 27.24.6 - Cycle-close reconciliation

Within the Mendlewick district, residential structures and education-overlay structures share the standing inspection cadence set out in Schedule I-2. The Site Marshal performs routine attestations at the cycle boundary, with discrepancies tracked by the Inspections Steward. This clause is procedural and does not impose category-level restrictions on operation.


### Clause 4.17.1 - Variance-application review

The Cobalthaven Municipal Authority records that heritage-listed activity in the Saltspire district is permitted under the standing schedule between 8:00 and 20:00 on any day of the week, subject to the routine attestation by the Inspections Steward. Activity outside these hours requires a temporary variance issued by the Zoning Analyst under Clause 28.11.1.


### Clause 10.23.20 - Standing-cadence confirmation

The Cobalthaven Municipal Authority records that industrial activity in the Wintergale district is permitted under the standing schedule between 8:00 and 19:00 on any day of the week, subject to the routine attestation by the Inspections Steward. Activity outside these hours requires a temporary variance issued by the Zoning Analyst under Clause 35.5.14.


### Clause 23.8.15 - Cycle-handover register

The Records Clerk confirms that the Northreach district's commercial overlay does NOT extend to waterfront-overlay structures, and that activities in waterfront-overlay structures within the same district are governed by Clause 15.12.15. Cross-overlay interactions are tracked by the Heritage Custodian and reviewed at the cycle close. This clause is informational.
